I, S. Chandramouli a male child born to Sundharam & Vanaja on 2nd May 1986, residing at No. 27, Muthu Nagar,
Appadurai Road, Thalakudi, Lalgudi Taluk, Tiruchirappalli-621 216 has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. Prof. Capt. S. Srinivasan Department of General Surgery Reg. No. 28456, Mahatma Gandhi
Medical College and Research Institute Pondy-Cuddalore Main Road, Pillaiyarkuppam, Pondicherry-607 402. By this I, may
be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as S. KARPAGARAKSHINI.

Tiruchirappalli,
16th February 2016.

S. CHANDRAMOULI.

Name of the Company

BALMER LAWRIE HIND TERMINALS PRIVATE LIMITED.

Warehousing and Logistic Services.

Date of appointment

:

By whom appointed

:

Members of the Company at the Extraordinary General

Chennai,
19th February 2016.

N. BALACHANDRAN,
Liquidator.

Notice is hereby given to the Public that the Members of M/S. BALMER LAWRIE HIND TERMINALS PRIVATE LIMITED
[hereinafter referred to as ‘the Company’ and having its registered office at Balmer Lawrie House, 628, Anna Salai,
Teynampet, Chennai-600 018], at the Extra Ordinary General Meeting held on 11th February 2016, has approved to
voluntarily liquidate the Company by passing the following resolution as “Special Resolution”:
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and having regard to
the Declaration of Solvency dated 8th January 2016, issued by the Board of Directors of the Company [which was
subsequently filed with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu, Chennai, on 9th February 2016] under Section 488 of the
Companies Act, 1956 [Wherein it has been stated that the Company has no debts, except winding-up/other expenses for
which necessary provision (s) has/have been made in the accounts] the consent of the Members of the Company, be and
is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the company as ‘Members’ Voluntary Winding up’, with immediate effect, i.e.
from 11-02-2016.”
The above said resolution and connected documents will be filed with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu,
Chennai, in due course.
Chennai,
19th February 2016.

PRABAL BASU,
Director.
